        // Filter query
        var sQueryFiltered = $("#site-search-1730436 input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#site-search-1730436 input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );

        if( $('#site-search-1730436-term').val() ){
            return true;
        }else{
            return false;
        }
    });

    <script>
     jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                        var sNavContainer = '#site-navbar-container';
                        var sBodyContainer = '.offcanvas-inner';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('DOMMouseScroll mousewheel', function(e){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
    </script>

                   </a>
                  </h3>

                 <div class="card-meta">

                <div class="card-headline">
                 <h3 class="tnt-headline">
                  <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/ads/sale/home/the-bruce-company---ad-from-2021-03-19/pdfdisplayad_1f70b110-1074-5a8c-8325-dc85fb05ef61.html">
                   THE BRUCE COMPANY - Ad from 2021-03-19
                  </a>
                 </h3>
                </div>
                <div class="card-meta">
                 <ul class="list-inline">
                  <li class="card-date">
                  </li>

           <script>
            jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                    var assetTracked = [];
                    var isUserAction = false;

                    function trackActive(owl){
                        if( assetTracked.length == 10 ){
                            return;
                        }else{
                            var activeThings = $(owl).find('.owl-item.active');

                            $.each(activeThings, function(index, value){
                                var assetId = $(this).find('.card').data('id');
                                var hasBeenLogged = false;
                                
                                assetTracked.forEach(function (item, index, array) {
                                    if(item == assetId){
                                        hasBeenLogged = true;
                                        return true;
                                    }
                                });
                                if( hasBeenLogged == false ){
                                    assetTracked.push(assetId);
                                    TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                                        app: 'classifieds',
                                        metric: 'featured',
                                        id: assetId
                                    });
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }

                    window.card_carousel_1730465 = $('#block-1730465 .owl-carousel');

                    card_carousel_1730465.on('initialized.owl.carousel', function(e){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_1730465);
                        });
                    
                    
                    card_carousel_1730465.owlCarousel({
                        autoplay:__tnt.client.touchOnly ? false : true,
                        autoplayTimeout:3000,
                        autoplayHoverPause:true,
                        loop:true,
                        margin:15,
                        nav:false,
                        dots:false,
                        slideBy: 'page',
                        autoHeight:false,
                        responsiveClass:true,
                        responsiveBaseElement: '#featured-classifieds-1730465',
                        responsive:{
                            0:{
                                items:1,
                                stagePadding: 40,
                                nav:false
                            },
                            600:{
                                items:1
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    // bind previous click
                    $('#block-1730465 .owl-carousel-control.prev').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_1730465.trigger('prev.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1730465);
                    });

                    // bind next click
                    $('#block-1730465 .owl-carousel-control.next').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_1730465.trigger('next.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1730465);
                    });

                    // bind dragged
                    card_carousel_1730465.on('dragged.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_1730465);
                    });

                    // bind translated
                    card_carousel_1730465.on('translated.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        if( isUserAction ){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_1730465);
                            isUserAction = false;
                        }
                    });
                });
           </script>
          </div>

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.tncmsTrackEvent));
            });
        });
  </script>
